statute prohemium iohannis rastell lawys real eglod wel statute iug metis decreys made wrytyn comynly freche toge dyuerse men thereof muse haue oft tymys comunicacio argumete cosyderig reason euery law wherto people shuld bo dyn oughte shuld wrytt n suche maner opynly publyssed decl yd people myght sone without gret di ficulte haue knowlege thesame lawes cause whithe said lawes eglod writi frech tog shuld seme fyrste vnknowyn wyllyam duke normandy came lande slewe kyng herrold conqueryd hole realm great nobre people wel gentilme cam vnderstode vulgar tong tyme vsyd realme onely frech tog also cause sayd kyng great wyse cou sel seiuid supposid vulgar tog w ich vsyd realme maner homely rude greate copy ad aboundauce wordys frenche tog tha vullgare tonge sel suffycyent expound declare matter lawis ordenauc thei hade determine made good gouernauce people effectually substauncyally cowd indyte frech tong therfore order wrote indited seid law made french tong forthermore longe comyng kynge wylya conquerour yt vse frech tog real began mynyssh dyuers people tha inhabytyd withi realm coud nother speke vulgare tongue realme nother french tong therfore wyse men realme causyd orderyd matter law accyos betwene te shuld pledyd shewyd defendyd answered debatyd uggyd englyssh vulgar tog ouer wryttyn enteryd recorde rollys latyn tonge cause euery man generally indyfferently myght haue knowlege thereof apperyth statute made xxxvi yere ed iii ca vltimo wherefore suppose caus rehersyd law realm idytid wrytti frech tog itedyd ryght good purpose yet besyde late day moste noble prynce late souereyn lorde kynge henry vii worthye called seconde salomon whiche excellyd polytyk wysedome pryncis reyngned realm tyme concyderynge well perseyuynge vulgare englissh tong maruelously amendyd augmentyd reason dyuerse famous clerkys lernyd men translate made many noble workys englisshe tog wherby moch plenty haboundance englyssh vsyd tymys past reaso ther vulgare tog aplified sufficient self expound lawys ordinaucis nedeful made ordre realm also thesame wyse price consyderyng vnyuersall people realm greate pleasure gaue theself greatly redynge vulgare englyssh tonge ordeynyd causyd statutys ordinauncis made commyn welth realm dayes shulde indytyd wryttyn vulgare englyssh tonge publysshyd declaryd impritid tha vnyuersally people realm myght sone haue knowleg sayd statut ordynau cys bound obserue reaso knowlege auoid dauger penaltes statutys also better lyffe tranquylyte pea dyscreyt charytable resonable order drad souereyne lord kyng henry viii hath co tynuyd folowyd causyd statutys haue made dayes also idytyd wrytten englyssh tonge intente lege people might haue knowleg ther goodly purposys intentys mynde ofte tymys reuoluyde hath causyd ake lytell payne translate frenche englysshe abbreuyacyon statutys fyrst yere reyn late uereyn lord kyng hen vii also thoughe statu made well tyme se kinge hen vii tyme souereyne lord suffyciently indytyd writen englysshe tong yet desyrouse shortly knowe effect tediouse rede thoughe mater effect copedyously abbreuiat wherfore farre symple wyt smal lernynge wyll extende haue takyn vppo abbregge effect shortly lytell book besechynge al syghte ther shall come accept gre though shall fortune fynde thynge eportyd omyttyd neglyges elli neclyges prynters yt wold lyke pardon consyder good wyl haue intendyd comi welth caus consyderacyons rehersyd also shal fortune dout poynte therof yet yf please maye resorte hole statute book bred gemente maner kalendre wyl aduertyse euery man shal fortune haue matter vre resort som ecclecia discooperta vel inde center ornata sirector petat decimas versus ochianos vel cotra rectorem dumodo petar quartapars alicuius ecclecie si rector petat mortuarium vell pensione oies huiusmodi faciend sint foro eccliastico de violent manuu iniecco clericum vel couersu vel causa de famacois alias cocessu fuit qd plitu inde tencatur curia cristianitat du modo non petatur pecunia si ad correconem peccati agat omnibus predictis casibus et consilibus habet dex eccilasticus congnoscere obsta te regia prohibicione si porrigat tractat de circumspecte agatis pwe hibit son churchis psume cut doune ani tree groweg church yard ther nedyth necessary byldyng reacyon channcell couertyd non vse statut edyt xiiii e ii pitem super oblacionibus obuenconibus non habet locu regia hibico et si clericus vel religiosus decimas suas congregatis vendiderit propecunia alicui si precium petatur cora iudice ecclesiastico locum habetregio prohibico si prelati imponant alicui penam corporalem si huiusmodi pena pro pe nnia redimatur locum habet regia prohibicio si coram prelatis vel episcopis pecunia exigatur psi quis manus violenter iniecerit clericu vel connersum pro violencia pacis debent fieri emende coram rege et pro excoicacoe coram epo velceteris prelatis imponatur p na corporalis qua si sponte reus velir redimere dado prelato vel leso pecunias potest nec talibus locus est regie hibicoi tractatu sub qua forma pin decimis oblacionibus obuencionibus mortuariis qn sub istis noibus proponuntur hibicoi regie est locus statut apud lincoln anno ix e ii voc articli cleri item si sit contencio de iure decemarum origin habes de iure potronatus earud deciarum quatitas excedat ad quartam partem bonoru ceclesie locum habeat regia prohibicio pitem si prelatus imponant penam pecuniariam alicui pro peccato et repetat illam locum habeat regia prohibicio sed si imponat penas corporales et si pu iti volunt huiusmodi penas propecuniis sponte redimere habet locum regia prohibicio si coram pecunia exigat eodem statuto pitem si causa vel negocia cuius recognico spectad foru ecclesiasticu cora ecclesiastico iudice fuerit sentencialit terminata et post modu coram iudice seculari super cadere iter easde asquestico moeatur r detur sic quado eade causa diuersis racionibus coram iudicibus ecclesiasticis et secularibus ventulatur vt supra patet de inieccione clericum dicut qd non obstante ecclesiastico iudico curia reg ipm tractat iudicium vt sibi videret expedire eodem staruto pedwardus c prelatis archidiaconis c c cognicones plintorum de transgressionibus et catallis et debitis que non sunt de testamento aut matrimonio ad coronam et dingnitatem nostram pertineant c vobis hibimus c c no super et aliis quorum cognico ad no pertinet parati sumus plenam iusticiam exibere incuria nostra madaus autem vicnostris quod premissa vobis alias nhibiant ex parte nostra et quod non mittant quod aliqui laici balliua sua aliquibus locis comoueant ad aliquas r congniciones per sacramenta sua facienda nisi causis matrimonialis et testament ariis et super huiusmodi feodis debitis et catallis coram vobis et aliis iudicibus ecclesiasticis premissis iurisdiccois nostre regie ad corona et dignitatem nostram spectantibus subire presumat et quicquid vos hac parte de feceri ti reddat no ad pleum cercores prohibicione formatta super articlis cleri pa proibicion giuen vppon
